[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         A critical security vulnerability has been detected in the Apache Commons Compress  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         library's `Expander` class. The fuzzer identified a file path traversal             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         vulnerability where the code attempts to write to a location outside the intended   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         target directory                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0m`[35m/tmp/expander-tmp2951478045293755397/output/q/r/[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m`[1m)[0m. This          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         vulnerability was caught by Jazzer's security sanitizer during fuzzing of the       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` functionality.                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ### Vulnerability Type                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         The issue is a **File Path Traversal** vulnerability [1m([0malso known as Directory       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Traversal or Path Traversal[1m)[0m, which is classified as a critical security issue.     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         This type of vulnerability allows an attacker to access files and directories that  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         are stored outside the intended directory structure.                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ### What the Issue Is                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         The stack trace shows that during the expansion of an archive file, the `Expander`  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         class in Apache Commons Compress attempted to create or write to a file path that   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         would result in directory traversal. The Jazzer security sanitizer detected this    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         behavior at `[1;35mFilePathTraversal.copyMismatchMvHook[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` and raised a                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` exception to prevent the traversal from occurring.    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         The problematic path                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[35m/tmp/expander-tmp2951478045293755397/output/q/r/[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m` suggests that:   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - A temporary directory was created at                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[35m/tmp/expander-tmp2951478045293755397/output/[0m`                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The extraction process attempted to write to a path containing                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `jazzer-traversal`, which likely indicates a test marker or specially crafted path  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         designed to escape the intended output directory                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The path components `q/r/` may represent directory structures from within the     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         archive being expanded                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ### Important Observations                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m. **Detection Point**: The vulnerability was caught at the                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[1;35mFilePathTraversal.copyMismatchMvHook[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` method, which indicates the issue occurs   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         during a file copy or move operation within the expansion process.                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m. **Call Chain**: The vulnerability originates from the following call sequence:   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - `[1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` [1m([0mline [1;36m216[0m[1m)[0m - Entry point                                   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m298[0m[39m:        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[95mcheck[0m[39m that the test file is defined correctly.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m299[0m[39m:        ZipFile zipFile = new [0m[1;35mZipFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39minput[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m300[0m[39m:        ZipArchiveEntry zae = [0m[1;35mzipFile.getEntry[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"a"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m301[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35massertNotNull[0m[1;39m([0m[39mzae[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m302[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35massertTrue[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mzae.isUnixSymlink[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m303[0m[39m:        byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m contents = new byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m304[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mIOUtils.readFully[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mzipFile.getInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mzae[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, contents[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m305[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35massertEquals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"b"[0m[39m, new [0m[1;35mString[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcontents[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m306[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m307[0m[39m:        zae = [0m[1;35mzipFile.getEntry[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"a/c/d/hello_world.txt"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m308[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35massertNotNull[0m[1;39m([0m[39mzae[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m309[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m310[0m[39m:        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[95mnow[0m[39m actually test that the file is written[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m311[0m[39m:        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[95mto[0m[39m the correct path[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m312[0m[39m:        new [0m[1;35mExpander[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[39minput, tmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m313[0m[39m:        Path target = [0m[1;35mtmp.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"b/c/d/hello_world.txt"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m314[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35massertTrue[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mFiles.isRegularFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtarget[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m315[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35massertEquals[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m13[0m[39m, [0m[1;35mFiles.size[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtarget[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m316[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Analysis Summary[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability is a **Path Traversal [0m[1;39m([0m[39mZip Slip[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m attack** enabled by a [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTime-of-Check to Time-of-Use [0m[1;39m([0m[39mTOCTOU[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m flaw combined with unsafe symbolic link [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfollowing in the ZipFile-specific expand method. [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Key Findings:**[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Root Cause**: The `createParentDirectory` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m508[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m524[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m follows [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msymbolic links [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m516[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and can return paths outside the target directory. After [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthis method is called, the target path is reassigned [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m497[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m500[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m WITHOUT [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mre-validation, bypassing the initial zip slip check at lines [0m[1;36m492[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m494[0m[39m.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Attack Vector**: [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Malicious archive creates a symlink entry pointing outside target directory [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m[32m"evil"[0m[39m → [0m[32m"../../../../tmp"[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Archive contains a file entry referencing the symlink [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"evil/malicious.txt"[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - During extraction, `createParentDirectory` follows the symlink to [0m[35m/[0m[95mtmp[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Target is reassigned to [0m[35m/tmp/[0m[95mmalicious.txt[0m[39m without validation[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - File is written outside the intended directory at line [0m[1;36m502[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Secondary Issues**:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Symlink creation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m477[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m489[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m doesn't validate symlink paths or targets[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Line [0m[1;36m480[0m[39m: `[0m[1;35mtargetDirectory.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mzae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` should use [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mzae.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirectory[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Line [0m[1;36m481[0m[39m: Symlink target is not validated to stay within targetDirectory[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Safe Alternatives**: Other archive formats [0m[1;39m([0m[39mTarFile, SevenZFile, [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mArchiveInputStream[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m use the generic expand method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m68[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m94[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m which:[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Uses `[0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` for proper path validation[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Uses `[0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` which doesn't follow symlinks[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Never reassigns paths after validation[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Comprehensive Fix Strategy[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mI will implement a **three-pronged fix** to address all vulnerability vectors while[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaintaining backward compatibility with legitimate symlink functionality:[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### **Part A: Fix Regular File Entry Processing [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLines [0m[1;36m490[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m504[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Replace vulnerable `createParentDirectory` with safe [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Files.createDirectories`**:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After initial validation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m492[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m494[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, use [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` instead of `createParentDirectory`[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This eliminates symlink following during directory creation[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove the entire path reassignment block [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m496[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m500[0m[1;39m)[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Simplify the flow**:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Validate target with existing check [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m492[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m494[0m[1;39m)[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Create parent directories safely with Files.createDirectories[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Write directly to validated target [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m502[0m[1;39m)[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### **Part B: Fix Symlink Entry Processing [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLines [0m[1;36m477[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m489[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Validate symlink path using `[0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`**:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace line [0m[1;36m480[0m[39m: `Path link = [0m[1;35mzae.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirectory[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This ensures the symlink itself stays within targetDirectory[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Validate symlink target path**:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After line [0m[1;36m481[0m[39m, add validation to ensure the target path stays within [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtargetDirectory[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Use the same `startsWith` check pattern: `if [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mtarget.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtargetDirectory.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Throw IOException if validation fails[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Simplify parent directory creation**:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace the complex `createParentDirectory` call [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m482[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlink.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove the reassignment logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m484[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m486[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m as it's no longer needed[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### **Part C: Remove or Fix `createParentDirectory` Method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLines [0m[1;36m508[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m524[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSince we're replacing all calls to this method with `Files.createDirectories`, we [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhave two options:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Option [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mRecommended[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: Remove the entire `createParentDirectory` method as [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mit's no longer used and is the source of the vulnerability.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Option [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mIf kept for backward compatibility[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: Fix it to validate the result:[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add validation after the loop to ensure `current` stays within `root`[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Throw IOException if the final path escapes root boundaries[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - However, since we're not using it anymore, removal is cleaner[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Implementation Details[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe patches will be applied to [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/examples/Expander.java`:[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Patch [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m - Fix Regular File Entry Processing [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround lines [0m[1;36m490[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m504[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**:[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCurrent vulnerable code:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m491[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m495[0m[39m: Initial validation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mKEEP[0m[1;39m)[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m496[0m[39m: createParentDirectory call [0m[1;39m([0m[39mREMOVE[0m[1;39m)[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Lines [0m[1;36m497[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m500[0m[39m: Path reassignment [0m[1;39m([0m[39mREMOVE[0m[1;39m)[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m501[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m503[0m[39m: File copy [0m[1;39m([0m[39mKEEP[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFixed code:[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Lines [0m[1;36m491[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m495[0m[39m: Initial validation [0m[1;39m([0m[39munchanged[0m[1;39m)[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- NEW: [0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Lines [0m[1;36m501[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m503[0m[39m: File copy to original validated target [0m[1;39m([0m[39munchanged[0m[1;39m)[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Patch [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m - Fix Symlink Entry Processing [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround lines [0m[1;36m477[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m489[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**:[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCurrent vulnerable code:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m480[0m[39m: [0m[1;35mtargetDirectory.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mzae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m481[0m[39m: [0m[1;35mtargetDirectory.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetName[0m[1;39m)[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m482[0m[39m: createParentDirectory call[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Lines [0m[1;36m484[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m486[0m[39m: Path reassignment[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Lines [0m[1;36m487[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m489[0m[39m: Symlink creation[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFixed code:[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m480[0m[39m: [0m[1;35mzae.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirectory[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - use safe resolution[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m481[0m[39m: [0m[1;35mtargetDirectory.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetName[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- NEW: Validate [0m[1;35mtarget.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtargetDirectory.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- NEW: [0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlink.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Lines [0m[1;36m487[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m489[0m[39m: Symlink creation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwith validated paths[0m[1;39m)[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Patch [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m - Remove createParentDirectory Method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m508[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m524[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**:[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mRemove the entire method as it's no longer used and is the vulnerability source[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification and Preservation[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why This is Optimal**:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Eliminates Root Cause**: Removes the unsafe symlink following in [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`createParentDirectory`[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Uses Standard Library**: `[0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is the standard, safe [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapproach that doesn't follow symlinks[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Maintains Validation**: Keeps the existing zip slip protection and adds proper[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msymlink validation[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Minimal Changes**: Only modifies the vulnerable ZipFile expand method, not the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msafe generic method[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Backward Compatible**: Continues to support legitimate symlinks [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtestSymLinks [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtest will pass[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Preserves Existing Logic**:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Path Traversal Tests**: All existing tests [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtestFileCantEscapeDoubleDotPath, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtestFileCantEscapeDoubleDotPathWithSimilarSibling, [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtestFileCantEscapeViaAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will continue to pass as we keep the initial [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidation[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Symlink Support**: The testSymLinks test will pass because we still create [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msymlinks, just with proper validation[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Other Formats**: No changes to TarFile, SevenZFile, or ArchiveInputStream [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethods - they remain safe[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Generic Expand**: The safe generic expand method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m68[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m94[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is untouched[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Addresses All Issues**:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **TOCTOU Vulnerability**: Eliminated by removing path reassignment after [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidation[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Symlink Following**: Eliminated by using `[0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` instead [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof custom logic[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Unvalidated Symlinks**: Fixed by using `[0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and adding target [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidation[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Code Complexity**: Reduced by removing complex parent directory logic[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential Side Effect [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m**: Symlinks with complex path relationships[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Mitigation**: The fix validates both symlink location and target, ensuring they[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstay within bounds while still supporting legitimate use cases like the [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtestSymLinks test[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential Side Effect [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m**: Archives with pre-existing directory symlinks[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Mitigation**: `[0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` will handle existing directories [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrectly, and symlink validation ensures malicious symlinks are rejected[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential Side Effect [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m**: Performance change[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Mitigation**: `[0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is likely faster than the custom [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`createParentDirectory` method, so performance should improve[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m. Similar Solutions in Codebase[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix follows the exact pattern already used safely in:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Generic expand method** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m68[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m94[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Uses `[0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` + [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **AbstractTest.java** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m156[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m168[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Reference implementation showing safe [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextraction[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Lister.java** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m51[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m61[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Another example of safe path handling[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis demonstrates that the fix aligns with established safe patterns in the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcodebase.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
